Vin yavlyaye soboyu odyn khto poslav Yoho kur'yeru z kerivnytstvom ta relihiyeyu pravdy, ta vstyhne dominate vsi relihiya, nezvazhayuchy na idola worshipers
O vy shcho vvazhayete, bahato relihiynykh lideriv ta propovidnykiv berete hroshi lyudey nezakonno, ta vyklykayete ohydu z shlyakhu BOHA. Tsey khto zapasayutʹ zoloto ta sriblo, ta ne vytrachayutʹ yikh v im'ya BOHA, obitsyayutʹ yim bolisnyy retribution

Tse yavlyaye soboyu doskonalu relihiyu; vy ne budete obrazyty vashi dushi (boryuchysʹ) pid chas Svyashchennykh Misyatsiv. Zmina Svyashchennykh Misyatsiv ye znak nadmirnoho disbelief; tse dodayetʹsya zbyvayuche z shlyakhu tsykh khto disbelieved. Vony zastupnyk Svyashchenni Misyatsi ta rehulyarni misyatsi, toy chas, yak zberihayuchy chyslo misyatsiv consecrated BOHOM. Vony takym chynom porushuyutʹ yakoho BOHA consecrated. Yakshcho vy ne spromozhetesʹ shchob pidtrymaty yoho (kur'yer), BOH vzhe pidtrymav yoho. Vy budete lehko mobilizuvaty, svitlo abo vazhke, ta dokladayete zusylʹ z vashymy hroshamy ta vashymy zhyttyam v im'ya BOHA. Tse ye krashche dlya vas, yakshcho vy tilʹky znaly

Pharaoh povernuvsya u tyrana na zemli, ta dyskryminuvav deyakykh lyudey. Vin peresliduvav bezporadnu hrupu z nykh, ubyvayuchy yikhnikh syniv, toy chas, yak ekonomyvshy yikhnikh dochok. Vin buv diysno bezputnyy

Zasudzhenyy yavlyayutʹ soboyu pratsi Abee Lahab, ta vin zasudzhuyetʹsya
Yoho hroshi ta shchob ni vin vykonanyy nikoly ne dopomozhe yomu
Vin pidpav palayuche Peklo
Takozh yoho druzhyna, khto pryviv persecution
